      try {
          function getUserThemePreference() {
            const themeInStorage = window.localStorage.getItem('theme');
            const systemTheme = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches ? 'dark' : 'light';

            const themes = {
              system: systemTheme,
              dark: 'dark',
              light: 'light'
            };

            return themes[themeInStorage] || systemTheme;
          };

          document.documentElement.setAttribute('data-theme', getUserThemePreference());
          document.body.dataset.theme = getUserThemePreference();
        } catch (error) {
          console.error(error);
        }
